CREATE TABLE InsertAirplane(
    AirplaneID VARCHAR(10) NOT NULL,
    Model VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL,
    RegistrationID	VARCHAR(10) NOT NULL,
    SeatCapacity NUMBER(3)	NOT NULL,
    TotalFlightTime	  NUMBER(10) NOT NULL,
    UnderMaintenance   VARCHAR(3) NOT NULL,
    UserID  VARCHAR(30),   
    TransDate  DATE,
    TransTime CHAR(8)
);

CREATE TABLE UpdateAirplane(
    AirplaneID		  VARCHAR(10)		NOT NULL,
    Model		  VARCHAR(20)		    NOT NULL,
    NewModel      VARCHAR(20)           NOT NULL,
    RegistrationID	  VARCHAR(10)		NOT NULL,
    NewRegistrationID	  VARCHAR(10)		NOT NULL,
    SeatCapacity	  NUMBER(3)	        NOT NULL,
    NewSeatCapacity	  NUMBER(3)	        NOT NULL,
    TotalFlightTime	  NUMBER(10)	        NOT NULL,
    NewTotalFlightTime	  NUMBER(10)	        NOT NULL,
    UnderMaintenance    VARCHAR(3)		NOT NULL,
    NewUnderMaintenance    VARCHAR(3)		NOT NULL,
    UserID         VARCHAR(30),   
    TransDate  DATE,
    TransTime CHAR(8)
);

    UnderMaintenance    VARCHAR(3)		NOT NULL,

    TransTime CHAR(8)
);

CREATE TABLE staff (
    StaffID       VARCHAR(10) NOT NULL,
    StaffName     VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    Gender        VARCHAR(1) NOT NULL,
    Phone          VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL,
    Role           VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL,
    FlightHour    NUMBER(10) DEFAULT 0,  
    Salary         NUMBER(10, 2) NOT NULL,  
    PRIMARY KEY (StaffID),
    CONSTRAINT chk_role CHECK (Role IN ('Pilot', 'Crew'))
);


CREATE TABLE promotion (
    PromotionID   VARCHAR(10) NOT NULL,
    PromotionName  VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    Detail         VARCHAR(120) NOT NULL,
    StartTime     DATE NOT NULL,
    EndTime       DATE NOT NULL,
    Discount        NUMBER(4,3) DEFAULT 0,
    PRIMARY KEY (PromotionID)
);


CREATE TABLE member (
    MemberID    VARCHAR(10) NOT NULL,
    MemberName  VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    Gender       VARCHAR(1) NOT NULL,
    Birthday     DATE NOT NULL,
    Email        VARCHAR(30) NOT NULL,
    Phone        VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL,
    MemberTier VARCHAR(10) DEFAULT 'Bronze',
    PRIMARY KEY (MemberID),
    CONSTRAINT chk_memberGender CHECK (Gender IN ('M', 'F')),
    CONSTRAINT chk_memberStatus CHECK (MemberTier IN ('Bronze', 'Silver', 'Gold', 'Platinum'))
);

Create TABLE Airplane(    
    AirplaneID		  VARCHAR(10)		NOT NULL,
    Model		  VARCHAR(20)		    NOT NULL,
    RegistrationID	  VARCHAR(10)		NOT NULL,
    SeatCapacity	  NUMBER(3)	        NOT NULL,
    TotalFlightTime	  NUMBER(10)	        NOT NULL,
    UnderMaintenance    VARCHAR(3)		NOT NULL,
    PRIMARY KEY (AirplaneID),
    CONSTRAINT chk_Maintenance CHECK (UnderMaintenance IN ('Yes', 'No'))
);

Create TABLE Parts(    
    PartsID	  	  VARCHAR(10)		NOT NULL,
    PartsName		  VARCHAR(15)		NOT NULL,
    QuantityInStock	  NUMBER(4)	,
    PriceEach 	  	  NUMBER(6,2)	    ,
    PRIMARY KEY (PartsID),
    CONSTRAINT chk_qty CHECK ((QuantityInStock >= 0))
);

Create TABLE Insurance(
	InsuranceID		VARCHAR(10)		NOT NULL,
	InsuranceCompany	VARCHAR(50)		NOT NULL,
	Detail			VARCHAR(100)			NOT NULL,
	Amount			NUMBER(10,2)		NOT NULL,
    PRIMARY KEY (InsuranceID)
);

Create TABLE Item(
	ItemID			VARCHAR(10)		NOT NULL,
	ItemName		VARCHAR(100)	NOT NULL,
	ItemType		VARCHAR(50)		NOT NULL,
    QuantityInStock NUMBER(4)       NOT NULL,
	Price			NUMBER(10, 2)	NOT NULL,
    PRIMARY KEY (ItemID)
);

Create TABLE Passenger(
	PassengerID		VARCHAR(10)		NOT NULL,
	PassengerName	VARCHAR(30)		NOT NULL,
	Gender			VARCHAR(1)		NOT NULL,
	IC			    VARCHAR(14)		NOT NULL,
	Email			VARCHAR(50)		NOT NULL,
	Phone			VARCHAR(15)		NOT NULL,
    PRIMARY KEY (PassengerID),
    CONSTRAINT chk_gender CHECK (Gender IN('M', 'F'))
);

CREATE TABLE booking(
    BookingID     varchar(10) NOT NULL,
    MemberID      varchar(10) ,
    StaffID       varchar(10) ,
    PromotionID   varchar(10) ,
    Booking_Date   TIMESTAMP(0) NOT NULL,
    Amount         number(10,2) DEFAULT 0,
    PRIMARY KEY (BookingID),
    FOREIGN KEY (MemberID) REFERENCES member(MemberID),
    FOREIGN KEY (StaffID) REFERENCES staff(StaffID),
    FOREIGN KEY (PromotionID) REFERENCES promotion(PromotionID)
);

Create TABLE FlightSchedule(    
    FlightID		VARCHAR(10)		NOT NULL,
    AirplaneID         VARCHAR(10)              NOT NULL,
    DepartureAirport	VARCHAR(3)		NOT NULL,
    ArrivalAirport	VARCHAR(3)		NOT NULL,
    DepartureTime	TIMESTAMP(0)	   NOT NULL,
    ArrivalTime	    TIMESTAMP(0)	    ,
    FlightDuration     NUMBER(10)		DEFAULT 0,
    FlightStatus       VARCHAR(10)		NOT NULL,
    PRIMARY KEY (FlightID), 
    FOREIGN KEY (AirplaneID) REFERENCES Airplane(AirplaneID),
    CONSTRAINT chk_FlightStatus CHECK (FlightStatus IN('Departed','Arrived','Delayed','Cancelled')),
    CONSTRAINT chk_FlightTime CHECK (DepartureTime < ArrivalTime)
);


Create TABLE Seats(    
    SeatsID	  	  VARCHAR(10)		NOT NULL,
    AirplaneID		  VARCHAR(10)		NOT NULL,
    SeatNumber	          VARCHAR(5)		NOT NULL,
    Class 	  	  VARCHAR(15)	        NOT NULL,
    Availability         VARCHAR(15)     DEFAULT 'Available',
    Price                NUMBER(6,2)         NOT NULL,
    PRIMARY KEY (SeatsID),
    FOREIGN KEY (AirplaneID) REFERENCES Airplane(AirplaneID),
    CONSTRAINT chk_Availability CHECK (Availability IN('Available','Booked','Reserved'))
);

Create TABLE Policy(
	PolicyID		VARCHAR(10)		NOT NULL,
	InsuranceID		VARCHAR(10)		NOT NULL,
	EffectiveDate	DATE			NOT NULL,
	ExpiryDate		DATE			NOT NULL,
	ClaimStatus		VARCHAR(15)		DEFAULT 'Not Claimed',
    PRIMARY KEY (PolicyID),
    FOREIGN KEY (InsuranceID) REFERENCES Insurance(InsuranceID),
    CONSTRAINT chk_ClaimStatus CHECK(ClaimStatus IN ('Claimed', 'Not Claimed'))
);

Create TABLE CheckIn(
    LuggageID		VARCHAR(10)		NOT NULL,
	PassengerID		VARCHAR(10)		NOT NULL,
	CheckInID		VARCHAR(10)		NOT NULL,
	CheckInTime		TIMESTAMP(0)	NOT NULL,
	Weight			NUMBER(6, 2)	NOT NULL,
	Status			VARCHAR(15)		NOT NULL,
    PRIMARY KEY (LuggageID),
    FOREIGN KEY (PassengerID) REFERENCES Passenger(PassengerID),
    CONSTRAINT chk_checkInStatus CHECK(Status IN('Checked-In', 'Rejected', 'Lost'))
);

Create TABLE ReportLost(
	ReportID		VARCHAR(10)		NOT NULL,
	LuggageID		VARCHAR(10)		NOT NULL,
	ReportTime		TIMESTAMP(0)	NOT NULL,
	Detail			VARCHAR(300)	NOT NULL,
	FoundStatus		VARCHAR(1)		DEFAULT 'N',
    PRIMARY KEY (ReportID),
    FOREIGN KEY (LuggageID) REFERENCES CheckIn(LuggageID),
    CONSTRAINT chk_foundStatus CHECK(FoundStatus IN('Y', 'N'))
);

Create TABLE Maintenance(    
    MaintenanceID	  VARCHAR(10)		NOT NULL,
    PartsID		  VARCHAR(10)		NOT NULL,
    AirplaneID	 	  VARCHAR(10)		NOT NULL,
    QuantityUsed	  NUMBER(3)	        NOT NULL,
    StartTime	  	  TIMESTAMP(0)          NOT NULL,
    EndTime    	  TIMESTAMP(0)		NOT NULL,
    Cost                 NUMBER(10,2)        DEFAULT NULL,
    PRIMARY KEY (MaintenanceID, PartsID),
    FOREIGN KEY (PartsID) REFERENCES Parts(PartsID),
    FOREIGN KEY (AirplaneID) REFERENCES Airplane(AirplaneID),
    CONSTRAINT chk_mainTime CHECK (StartTime < EndTime)
);

Create TABLE Purchase(
	PassengerID		VARCHAR(10)		NOT NULL,
	ItemID			VARCHAR(10)		NOT NULL,
	Quantity		NUMBER(3)			NOT NULL,
	PurchaseDate	TIMESTAMP(0)			NOT NULL,
	Amount			NUMBER(10,2)		DEFAULT NULL,
    PRIMARY KEY (PassengerID, ItemID),
    FOREIGN KEY (PassengerID) REFERENCES Passenger(PassengerID),
    FOREIGN KEY (ItemID) REFERENCES Item(ItemID)
);


Create TABLE WorkAllocation(
	StaffID		        VARCHAR(10)		NOT NULL,
	FlightID		VARCHAR(10)		NOT NULL,
	ClockInTime		TIMESTAMP(0)		NOT NULL,
	ClockOutTime	TIMESTAMP(0)		NOT NULL,
	WorkHour		NUMBER(3)			DEFAULT NULL,
    PRIMARY KEY (StaffID, FlightID),
    FOREIGN KEY (StaffID) REFERENCES Staff(StaffID),
    FOREIGN KEY (FlightID) REFERENCES FlightSchedule(FlightID)
);

CREATE TABLE BookingDetail(
    BookingID   VARCHAR(10)     NOT NULL,
    PassengerID VARCHAR(10)     NOT NULL,
    WayID       NUMBER(1)       NOT NULL,
    FlightID    VARCHAR(10)     NOT NULL,
    SeatsID      VARCHAR(10)     NOT NULL,
    CheckInID VARCHAR(10)       NOT NULL,
    PolicyID    VARCHAR(10)     NOT NULL,
    Status      VARCHAR(10)     NOT NULL,
    PRIMARY KEY (BookingID, PassengerID, WayID),
    FOREIGN KEY (PassengerID) REFERENCES Passenger(PassengerID),
    FOREIGN KEY (FlightID) REFERENCES FlightSchedule(FlightID),
    FOREIGN KEY (SeatsID) REFERENCES Seats(SeatsID),
    FOREIGN KEY (PolicyID) REFERENCES Policy(PolicyID),
    CONSTRAINT chk_bookDetailStatus CHECK (Status IN ('Success','Cancelled'))
);

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
CREATE OR REPLACE TRIGGER trg_newPurchase
BEFORE INSERT ON Purchase
FOR EACH ROW
DECLARE
    v_qty_in_stock NUMBER;
    v_price_each NUMBER;
    v_total_price NUMBER;
BEGIN
    SELECT QuantityInStock, Price
    INTO v_qty_in_stock, v_price_each
    FROM Item
    WHERE ItemID = :NEW.ItemID;
    
    IF :NEW.Quantity <= v_qty_in_stock  THEN
        v_total_price := v_price_each * :NEW.Quantity;
        
        UPDATE Item
        SET QuantityInStock = QuantityInStock - :NEW.Quantity
        WHERE ItemID = :NEW.ItemID;
        
        :NEW.Amount := v_total_price;
    ELSE 
        RAISE_APPLICATION_ERROR(-20000, 'Insufficient stock for item: ' || :NEW.ItemID);
    END IF; 
   
END;
/

CREATE OR REPLACE TRIGGER trg_newMaintenance
BEFORE INSERT ON Maintenance
FOR EACH ROW
DECLARE
    v_qty_in_stock NUMBER;
    v_price_each NUMBER;
    v_total_price NUMBER;
BEGIN
    SELECT QuantityInStock, PriceEach
    INTO v_qty_in_stock, v_price_each
    FROM Parts
    WHERE PartsID = :NEW.PartsID;
    
    IF :NEW.QuantityUsed <= v_qty_in_stock  THEN
        v_total_price := v_price_each * :NEW.QuantityUsed;
        
        UPDATE Parts
        SET QuantityInStock = QuantityInStock - :NEW.QuantityUsed
        WHERE PartsID = :NEW.PartsID;
        
        :NEW.Cost := v_total_price;
    ELSE 
        RAISE_APPLICATION_ERROR(-20000, 'Insufficient stock for part: ' || :NEW.PartsID);
    END IF; 
   
END;
/

CREATE OR REPLACE TRIGGER trg_calcWorkHour
BEFORE INSERT OR UPDATE ON WorkAllocation
FOR EACH ROW 
BEGIN
    :NEW.WorkHour := ROUND(
                (EXTRACT(DAY FROM (:NEW.ClockOutTime - :NEW.ClockInTime)) * 24) +
                EXTRACT(HOUR FROM (:NEW.ClockOutTime - :NEW.ClockInTime))
            );
END;
/

CREATE OR REPLACE TRIGGER trg_calcFlight
AFTER INSERT OR UPDATE ON WorkAllocation
FOR EACH ROW
DECLARE 
    v_status    VARCHAR(10);
    v_arrival       TIMESTAMP(0);
    v_departure     TIMESTAMP(0);
    v_flightDuration NUMBER(10);
    v_WorkHour NUMBER(10);
BEGIN
    SELECT FlightStatus into v_status 
    FROM FlightSchedule 
    WHERE FlightID = :NEW.FlightID;

    IF (v_status = 'Arrived') THEN
        SELECT ArrivalTime, DepartureTime INTO v_arrival, v_departure
        FROM FlightSchedule 
        WHERE FlightID = :NEW.FlightID;

        v_flightDuration := ROUND(
            (CAST(v_arrival AS DATE) - CAST(v_departure AS DATE)) * 24 
        );

        UPDATE FlightSchedule
        SET FlightDuration = v_flightDuration
        WHERE FlightID = :NEW.FlightID;

        UPDATE Staff 
        SET FlightHour = FlightHour + v_flightDuration
        WHERE StaffID = :New.StaffID;

    ELSE 
        UPDATE FlightSchedule 
        SET ArrivalTime = NULL
        WHERE FlightID = :NEW.FlightID;
    END IF;
END;
/


--yy
CREATE OR REPLACE TRIGGER trg_calcBookPrice 
AFTER INSERT OR UPDATE ON BookingDetail 
FOR EACH ROW 
DECLARE 
    v_bookTime TIMESTAMP(0);
    v_seat  NUMBER(6,2);
    v_purchase NUMBER(10,2);
    v_insurance NUMBER(10,2);
    v_promotion NUMBER(4,3);
    v_total NUMBER(10,2);
BEGIN 
    -- Get the seat price
    BEGIN
        SELECT Price INTO v_seat
        FROM Seats
        WHERE SeatsID = :NEW.SeatsID;
    EXCEPTION
        WHEN NO_DATA_FOUND THEN
            v_seat := 0;
    END;

    -- Get the booking time
    BEGIN
        SELECT Booking_Date INTO v_bookTime
        FROM Booking 
        WHERE BookingID = :NEW.BookingID;
    EXCEPTION
        WHEN NO_DATA_FOUND THEN
            v_bookTime := NULL;
    END;

    -- Sum the purchase amounts for the given passenger at the booking time
    BEGIN
        SELECT COALESCE(SUM(P.Amount), 0) INTO v_purchase
        FROM Purchase P
        WHERE P.PassengerID = :NEW.PassengerID
        AND P.PurchaseDate = v_bookTime;
    EXCEPTION
        WHEN NO_DATA_FOUND THEN
            v_purchase := 0;
    END;

    -- Get the insurance amount
    BEGIN
        SELECT amount INTO v_insurance
        FROM Policy PL, Insurance INS
        WHERE PL.InsuranceID = INS.InsuranceID
        AND PL.PolicyID = :NEW.PolicyID;
    EXCEPTION
        WHEN NO_DATA_FOUND THEN
            v_insurance := 0;
    END;

    -- Get the promotion discount
    BEGIN
        SELECT COALESCE(PM.Discount, 0) INTO v_promotion
        FROM Promotion PM, Booking B 
        WHERE PM.PromotionID = B.PromotionID
        AND B.BookingID = :NEW.BookingID;
    EXCEPTION
        WHEN NO_DATA_FOUND THEN
            v_promotion := 0;
    END;

    -- Calculate the total amount
    v_total := (v_seat + v_purchase + v_insurance) * (1 - v_promotion);

    -- Update the booking amount
    UPDATE Booking 
    SET Amount = v_total
    WHERE BookingID = :NEW.BookingID;
END;
/

CREATE OR REPLACE TRIGGER PreventOverlappingMaintenance
BEFORE INSERT ON Maintenance
FOR EACH ROW
DECLARE
    v_count NUMBER;
BEGIN
    SELECT COUNT(*)
    INTO v_count
    FROM Maintenance
    WHERE AirplaneID = :NEW.AirplaneID
    AND ((:NEW.StartTime BETWEEN StartTime AND EndTime)
    OR (:NEW.EndTime BETWEEN StartTime AND EndTime)
    OR (:NEW.StartTime < StartTime AND :NEW.EndTime > EndTime));
    
    IF v_count > 0 THEN
        RAISE_APPLICATION_ERROR(-20000, 'Overlapping maintenance operation detected.');
    END IF;
END;
/

CREATE OR REPLACE TRIGGER trg_track_Member
AFTER INSERT OR UPDATE OR DELETE ON Member
FOR EACH ROW
BEGIN      	
 CASE
  WHEN INSERTING THEN
    INSERT INTO InsertMember
    VALUES (:NEW.MemberID, :NEW.MemberName, :NEW.Gender, :NEW.Birthday, :NEW.Email, 
    :NEW.Phone, :NEW.MemberTier, USER, SYSDATE, TO_CHAR(SYSDATE, 'HH24:MI:SS'));
  WHEN UPDATING THEN
    INSERT INTO UpdateMember
    VALUES (:OLD.MemberID, :OLD.MemberName, :NEW.MemberName, :OLD.Gender, :NEW.Gender, 
    :OLD.Birthday, :NEW.Birthday, :OLD.Email, :NEW.Email, :OLD.Phone, :NEW.Phone, 
    :OLD.MemberTier, :NEW.MemberTier, USER, SYSDATE, TO_CHAR(SYSDATE, 'HH24:MI:SS'));

  WHEN DELETING THEN
    INSERT INTO DeleteMember
    VALUES (:OLD.MemberID, :OLD.MemberName, :OLD.Gender, :OLD.Birthday, :OLD.Email, 
    :OLD.Phone, :OLD.MemberTier, USER, SYSDATE, TO_CHAR(SYSDATE, 'HH24:MI:SS'));
 END CASE;
END;
/

CREATE OR REPLACE TRIGGER trg_track_Staff
AFTER INSERT OR UPDATE OR DELETE ON Staff
FOR EACH ROW
BEGIN      	
 CASE
  WHEN INSERTING THEN
    INSERT INTO InsertStaff
    VALUES (:NEW.StaffID, :NEW.StaffName, :NEW.Gender, :NEW.Phone, :NEW.Role,
    :NEW.FlightHour, :NEW.Salary, USER, SYSDATE, TO_CHAR(SYSDATE, 'HH24:MI:SS'));

  WHEN UPDATING THEN
    INSERT INTO UpdateStaff
    VALUES (:OLD.StaffID, :OLD.StaffName, :NEW.StaffName, :OLD.Gender, :NEW.Gender, 
    :OLD.Phone, :NEW.Phone, :OLD.Role, :NEW.Role, :OLD.FlightHour, :NEW.FlightHour, 
    :OLD.Salary, :NEW.Salary, USER, SYSDATE, TO_CHAR(SYSDATE, 'HH24:MI:SS'));

  WHEN DELETING THEN
    INSERT INTO DeleteStaff
    VALUES (:OLD.StaffID, :OLD.StaffName, :OLD.Gender, :OLD.Phone, :OLD.Role, 
    :OLD.FlightHour, :OLD.Salary, USER, SYSDATE, TO_CHAR(SYSDATE, 'HH24:MI:SS'));
 END CASE;
END;
/

CREATE OR REPLACE TRIGGER trg_track_Promotion
AFTER INSERT OR UPDATE OR DELETE ON Promotion
FOR EACH ROW
BEGIN      	
 CASE
  WHEN INSERTING THEN
    INSERT INTO InsertPromotion
    VALUES (:NEW.PromotionID, :NEW.PromotionName, :NEW.Detail, :NEW.StartTime, :NEW.EndTime, 
    :NEW.Discount, USER, SYSDATE, TO_CHAR(SYSDATE, 'HH24:MI:SS'));
  WHEN UPDATING THEN
    INSERT INTO UpdatePromotion
    VALUES (:OLD.PromotionID, :OLD.PromotionName, :NEW.PromotionName, :OLD.Detail,:NEW.Detail, :OLD.StartTime,:NEW.StartTime, :OLD.EndTime, 
    :NEW.EndTime, :OLD.Discount,:NEW.Discount, USER, SYSDATE, TO_CHAR(SYSDATE, 'HH24:MI:SS'));

  WHEN DELETING THEN
    INSERT INTO DeletePromotion
    VALUES (:OLD.PromotionID, :OLD.PromotionName, :OLD.Detail, :OLD.StartTime, :OLD.EndTime, 
    :OLD.Discount, USER, SYSDATE, TO_CHAR(SYSDATE, 'HH24:MI:SS'));
 END CASE;
END;
/

CREATE OR REPLACE TRIGGER trg_track_Item
AFTER INSERT OR UPDATE OR DELETE ON Item
FOR EACH ROW
BEGIN      	
 CASE
  WHEN INSERTING THEN
    INSERT INTO InsertItem
    VALUES (:NEW.ItemID, :NEW.ItemName, :NEW.ItemType, :NEW.QuantityInStock, :NEW.Price, 
    USER, SYSDATE, TO_CHAR(SYSDATE, 'HH24:MI:SS'));
  WHEN UPDATING THEN
    INSERT INTO UpdateItem
    VALUES (:OLD.ItemID, :OLD.ItemName, :NEW.ItemName, :OLD.ItemType, :NEW.ItemType, 
    :OLD.QuantityInStock, :NEW.QuantityInStock, :OLD.Price, :NEW.Price,
    USER, SYSDATE, TO_CHAR(SYSDATE, 'HH24:MI:SS'));

  WHEN DELETING THEN
    INSERT INTO DeleteItem
    VALUES (:OLD.ItemID, :OLD.ItemName, :OLD.ItemType, :OLD.QuantityInStock, :OLD.Price, 
    USER, SYSDATE, TO_CHAR(SYSDATE, 'HH24:MI:SS'));
 END CASE;
END;
/

CREATE OR REPLACE TRIGGER trg_track_Airplane
AFTER INSERT OR UPDATE OR DELETE ON Airplane
FOR EACH ROW
BEGIN      	
 CASE
  WHEN INSERTING THEN
    INSERT INTO InsertAirplane
    VALUES (:NEW.AirplaneID, :NEW.Model, :NEW.RegistrationID, :NEW.SeatCapacity, :NEW.TotalFlightTime, 
    :NEW.UnderMaintenance, USER, SYSDATE, TO_CHAR(SYSDATE, 'HH24:MI:SS'));
  WHEN UPDATING THEN
    INSERT INTO UpdateAirplane
    VALUES (:OLD.AirplaneID, :OLD.Model, :NEW.Model, :OLD.RegistrationID, :NEW.RegistrationID, 
    :OLD.SeatCapacity, :NEW.SeatCapacity, :OLD.TotalFlightTime, :NEW.TotalFlightTime, :OLD.UnderMaintenance, :NEW.UnderMaintenance, 
    USER, SYSDATE, TO_CHAR(SYSDATE, 'HH24:MI:SS'));

  WHEN DELETING THEN
    INSERT INTO DeleteAirplane
    VALUES (:OLD.AirplaneID, :OLD.Model, :OLD.RegistrationID, :OLD.SeatCapacity, :OLD.TotalFlightTime, 
    :OLD.UnderMaintenance, USER, SYSDATE, TO_CHAR(SYSDATE, 'HH24:MI:SS'));
 END CASE;
END;
/

DROP INDEX member_name_idx;
CREATE INDEX member_name_idx ON MEMBER (UPPER(MemberName));

DROP INDEX item_name_idx;
CREATE INDEX item_name_idx ON Item (UPPER(ItemName));

DROP INDEX parts_name_idx;
CREATE INDEX parts_name_idx ON Parts (UPPER(PartsName));

DROP INDEX staff_name_idx;
CREATE INDEX satff_name_idx ON Staff (UPPER(StaffName));

DROP INDEX passenger_name_idx;
CREATE INDEX passenger_name_idx ON Passenger (UPPER(PassengerName));
